     <script type="text/javascript">
      function mcEvilPopupClose(){
 	jQuery('#mc_embed_signup').fadeOut();
 	var now = new Date();
 	var expires_date = new Date( now.getTime() + 31536000000 );
 	document.cookie = 'MCEvilPopupClosed=yes;expires=' + expires_date.toGMTString()+';path=/';
 }
 jQuery(document).ready( function() {
 	var date=new Date();
 	var datetime=(date.getMonth()+1)+'/'+date.getDate()+'/'+date.getFullYear();
 	if(document.cookie.indexOf('MCEvilPopupClosed')== -1 ){
 		jQuery('#mc_embed_signup').fadeIn();
 	}
 	jQuery('#mc_embed_close').click(function(){mcEvilPopupClose();});
 	jQuery(document).keydown(function(e){
 		if (e == null) { 
 			keycode = event.keyCode;
 		} else { 
 			keycode = e.which;
 		}
 		if(keycode == 27){
 			mcEvilPopupClose();
 		}
 	});
 });
     </script>

     <div class="product-slider" id="about_us">
      <h4 class="slider-title">
       About Us
      </h4>
      <div class="clear">
      </div>
      <hr style="margin: 0 0 5px;"/>
      <p>
       Welcome to Elegant Wedding Invites! We are an online
       <span style="color: #ef6356;">
        <a href="/shop/wedding-invitations-2/">
         <span style="color: #ef6356;">
          <span style="color: #000000;">
           cheap wedding invitations
          </span>
         </span>
        </a>
       </span>
       shop specializing in stylish and chic wedding invitations all designs printed on your choice of three kinds of stock card. Elegant Wedding Invites offers a variety of styles including
       <a href="/shop/modern_wedding-invitations/">
        modern
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/shop/peacock-wedding_invitations/">
        peacock
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/shop/vintage-wedding_invites/">
        vintage
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/shop/rustic_wedding-invitations/">
        rustic
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/shop/watercolor-wedding-invitations-online/">
        watercolor
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/shop/pocket-invites/">
        pocket wedding invitations
       </a>
       . Browse our collection through seasons like
       <a href="/shop/invitation-for-fall-and-autumn-wedding/">
        fall
       </a>
       , or by type of venue like
       <a href="/shop/beach_wedding-invitations/">
        beach
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/shop/destination-wedding_invites/">
        destination wedding invitations
       </a>
       . There are also
       <a href="/shop/unique-wedding_invites/">
        unique wedding invitations
       </a>
       , at Elegant Wedding Invites, which are hand drawn styles that can be personalized to your personality and uniqueness. Or if you’re unsure about what you want, why not send us some photos of you and your dashing fiancé and we’ll make some exclusive
       <a href="/shop/photo_wedding-invitations/">
        photo wedding invitations
       </a>
       just for you. If you cannot find the right invitation design or color from our extensive catalogue range then don’t worry; we are now providing free color and design custom service. Please feel free to
       <a href="/contact-us/">
        contact us
       </a>
       should you have any problems.
      </p>
